## Template Definitions

| Template | Description | en_us Count |
|----------|-------------|-------------|
| `template-home` | Full-featured marketing/landing pages with hero, carousels, etc. | 158 |
| `template-product-catalog` | Product listing/catalog pages | 1 |
| `template-product-detail` | Individual product specification and detail pages | 716 |
| `template-application-catalog` | Application catalog entries | 112 |
| `template-about` | Corporate, legal, career, customer story, and informational pages | 141 |
| `template-engage` | Campaign and engagement landing pages | 29 |
| `specialized` | Support portals, community forums, software downloads, utilities | 42 |
| `template-about (investors)` | Investor relations pages | 9 |
| *newsroom* | Press releases and news articles | 2009 |
